If events keep\\n57: \\t// showing up with no break for this time, we'll trigger a push.\\n58: \\tdebounceMax time.Duration\\n59: \\n60: \\t// enableEDSDebounce indicates whether EDS pushes should be debounced.\\n61: \\tenableEDSDebounce bool\\n62: }\\n63: \\n64: // DiscoveryServer is Pilot's gRPC implementation for Envoy's xds APIs\\n65: type DiscoveryServer struct {\\n66: \\t// Env is the model environment.\\n67: \\tEnv *model.Environment\\n68: \\n69: \\t// Generators allow customizing the generated config, based on the client metadata.\\n70: \\t// Key is the generator type - will match the Generator metadata to set the per-connection\\n71: \\t// default generator, or the combination of Generator metadata and TypeUrl to select a\\n72: \\t// different generator for a type.\\n73: \\t// Normal istio clients use the default generator - will not be impacted by this.\\n74: \\tGenerators map[string]model.XdsResourceGenerator\\n75: \\n76: \\t// ProxyNeedsPush is a function that determines whether a push can be completely skipped. \\n137: \\tkrtDebugger *krt.DebugHandler\\n138: }\\n139: \\n140: // NewDiscoveryServer creates DiscoveryServer that sources data from Pilot's internal mesh data structures\\n141: func
